Summary of changes between TrueOS 17.12 and 18.03 
----------------
New Packages: 2461
Removed Packages: 829
Updated Packages: 2984

Notes about package statistics:
* Some packages that have been renamed between releases (such as the KDE4 packages) will show up on both the removed list (old name) and the new list (new name) simultaneously.
* Many of the new packages are due to the new “flavor” system being activated for python-based ports. This means that many of those applications now have two packages available, one for python 2.7 (py27-*) and one for python 3.6 (py36-*).
* The list of updated packages does not include those where the port revision is the only thing that has changed. It only accounts for an actual change in the upstream version of the package.
